      <h4 class="section2 ms-alternating" id="section-6">Resident Status</h4> 
      <dl> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> I already submitted my SIR. Isn’t that the same as the SLR? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>No. The SIR is your “Statement of Intent to Register.” It indicates that you are planning to attend UCR. The SLR is your “Statement of Legal Residence.” It indicates your resident or non-resident status. You can only submit your SLR after you have submitted your SIR. See <a href="../tuition-and-fees/residency-for-tuition-purposes.aspx">Residency for Tuition Purposes</a> for more details.</p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> SIR vs SLR 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>The SIR is your “Statement of Intent to Register.” It indicates that you are planning to attend UCR. The SLR is your “Statement of Legal Residence.” It indicates your resident or non-resident status. You can only submit your SLR after you have submitted your SIR. See <a href="../tuition-and-fees/residency-for-tuition-purposes.aspx">Residency for Tuition Purposes</a> for more details.</p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> How do I know if I am determined to be a resident for tuition purposes? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>After you submit your online SLR, we will review it and make a determination. If we need additional information or documents, we will contact you via your personal email, prior to July 1. After July 1, all emails will be sent to your UCR R’Mail account.</p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> Am I considered a California resident? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>There are four residence requirements you must meet in order to qualify for California resident status. <a href="http://www.ucop.edu/general-counsel/guidance/educational-affairs-and-campus-services/residence-tuition-fees-student-info.html#residence-requirements">See them here. </a></p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> How is residency determined? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>After you submit your online SLR, we will review it and make a determination. If we need additional information or documents, we will contact you via your personal email, prior to July 1. After July 1, all emails will be sent to your UCR R’Mail account.</p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> What is the difference between the SLR and SIR? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>The SIR is your “Statement of Intent to Register.” It indicates that you are planning to attend UCR. The SLR is your “Statement of Legal Residence.” It indicates your resident or non-resident status. You can only submit your SLR after you have submitted your SIR. See <a href="../tuition-and-fees/residency-for-tuition-purposes.aspx">Residency for Tuition Purposes</a> for more details.</p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> I will not be living in the dorms. Do I still need to submit the SLR? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>Yes. The SLR is to determine your residency for tuition purposes. It is not related to your choice to live or not live in the residence halls. </p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> I am a resident because I’ve lived here all my life. Do I still need to fill out the form? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>Yes. Every student must submit the online SLR, regardless of where you have lived or how long you have been in California. The only exception to this is if you log in to your MyUCR account, click the “Statement of Legal Residency” link and see the California bear flag badge. If you see this, you do not need to complete the form as you have already answered the required questions on the UC admissions application. </p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> The Office of Admissions already declared me a resident. Do I still need to submit the SLR? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>Yes. The Office of Admissions’ determination only pertains to your GPA and test scores, not to <a href="../tuition-and-fees/residency-for-tuition-purposes.aspx">Residency for Tuition Purposes.</a></p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> I have F1 visa status. Am I eligible for resident tuition? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>No. An F1 visa is a student visa and is only valid for a specific reason and for a specific amount of time. This prohibits an F1 visa holder from establishing <a href="../tuition-and-fees/residency-for-tuition-purposes.aspx">Residency for Tuition Purposes.</a> For more information, please contact the International Education Center. </p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> I was considered a resident at my community college. Does that mean I’m a resident at UCR 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>No. Some students transferring from community colleges may receive a different classification at UCR. Most often it is because their parents are from out of state and do not meet UC requirements for financial independence. See <a href="../tuition-and-fees/residency-for-tuition-purposes.aspx">Residency for Tuition Purposes</a> for more information.</p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> What happens if I don’t fill out the SLR? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>You will be classified “undetermined” and automatically charged the higher, non-resident tuition rate. </p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> I live in the dorms. Am I a resident? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>Not necessarily. Please see <a href="../tuition-and-fees/residency-for-tuition-purposes.aspx">Residency for Tuition Purposes</a> for more information.</p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> What is “Residency for Tuition and Fee Purposes”? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>Your residency status (whether you are a California resident or not) is dependent on whether your tuition and fees will be charged at a California-resident or nonresident rate. Our campus residence affairs officer determines that status based on information you provide in your Statement of Legal Residence. See <a href="../tuition-and-fees/residency-for-tuition-purposes.aspx">Residency for Tuition and Fee Purposes</a> for more details.</p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> What is the Statement of Legal Residence (SLR)? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>The SLR is how you declare your residency status when you first come to UCR (as a freshman, transfer or graduate student) or when you return after a significant break (longer than three quarters). You submit it along with your Statement of Intent to Register.<br /><br />Additional documentation may be required to prove your status. You have until the end of the applicable term to provide it. Freshmen and transfer students who have submitted their Statement of Intent to Register will be able to access the SLR via their MyUCR account. Graduate students will receive a packet from Graduate Admissions.<br /><br />See<a href="../tuition-and-fees/residency-for-tuition-purposes.aspx"> Residency for Tuition and Fee Purposes </a>for more details.</p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> How do I establish residency? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>You should aim for meeting the four residence requirements outlined <a href="http://www.ucop.edu/general-counsel/guidance/educational-affairs-and-campus-services/residence-tuition-fees-student-info.html#residence-requirements">here</a>. </p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> My residency status changed, what do I do? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>If your residency status changed, you must immediately notify the campus residence affairs officer: <a href="mailto:Kendra.McCann@ucr.edu">Kendra.McCann@ucr.edu</a> </p>
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> I am now a resident. How do I change my status? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>If you want to be classified as a resident, you must petition in person at our office. All status changes must be initiated before the first day of classes for the applicable term. Our office is located on the second floor of the Student Services Building, Room 2249. For in-person service, students should start at the Highlander One Stop Shop (HOSS) on the first floor of the Student Services Building. Office hours are Monday through Friday, 9 a.m. – 5 p.m.</p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> My residency was classified incorrectly, what do I do? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>If your resident status was classified incorrectly, you must immediately notify the campus residence affairs officer (<a href="mailto:Kendra.McCann@ucr.edu">Kendra.McCann@ucr.edu</a>). If you were incorrectly classified as a resident, you are subject to nonresident tuition. If you concealed or gave false information, you may be subject to university discipline.</p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> Can I appeal a resident status decision? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>Students denied resident status might have the right to appeal. Appeals must be filed within 30 days of notification of the campus residence affairs officer’s decision. Download<a href="http://www.ucop.edu/general-counsel/_files/ed-affairs/uc-residency-instructions-appeal-form.pdf"> the Instructions and Application to Appeal a Nonresident Classification.<br /> </a></p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> Who do I talk to about California residency? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>All inquiries should be directed to:<br /><br />Kendra McCann<br />Residence Affairs Officer<br />Office of the Registrar<br />2249 Student Services Building<br /><a href="mailto:Kendra.McCann@ucr.edu">Kendra.McCann@ucr.edu</a><br />951-827-5970<br /><br />No other university personnel are authorized to supply information connected to residency for tuition and fee purposes.</p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> Who do I talk to about residency status? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>All inquiries should be directed to:<br /><br />Kendra McCann<br />Residence Affairs Officer<br />Office of the Registrar<br />2249 Student Services Building<br /><a href="mailto:Kendra.McCann@ucr.edu">Kendra.McCann@ucr.edu</a><br />951-827-5970<br /><br />No other university personnel are authorized to supply information connected to residency for tuition and fee purposes.</p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> Am I eligible for the AB540 nonresident tuition exemption? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>Domestic students who, for various reasons, are classified as nonresidents, as well as undocumented students, may be eligible. An example of a potentially eligible nonresident domestic student is one who attended a California high school for three or more years and graduated from one, but parents did not live in California or later moved away.<br /><br />Students who met in-state criteria and then established residency in another state, but are now returning to California to pursue a graduate degree, may also be eligible for the tuition exemption. The exemption applies to both undergraduate and graduate students.<br /><br />Graduate students must provide an official high school transcript to the Registrar’s Office. Undergraduate (freshman and transfer) students may provide an official high school transcript as well; however, we will attempt to obtain a copy of it from Undergraduate Admissions.<br /><br />Most importantly, all students must complete their SLR (Statement of Legal Residence) online before sending us any documents.</p> 
       </dd> 
       <a class="btt" href="#top">Back to Top</a> 
      </dl> 
      <h4 class="section2 ms-alternating" id="section-7">Miscellaneous</h4> 
      <dl> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> What is considered a “business day”? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>Any day our office is open for business is considered a business day. Non-business days are Saturday and Sunday, holidays and administrative closure dates. Enrollment verifications take five to seven business days to process. </p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> How do I calculate my GPA? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>First, calculate grade points by multiplying the value (V) of an assigned grade by the unit value (UV) of the course (grade points = V x UV). The grade point average (GPA) requires two sums: the sum of all the grade points earned for the term you are calculating (quarter points [QPTS]) and the sum of all the letter-graded units attempted during the term (quarter hours [QHRS]). To determine the GPA, divide the quarter points by the quarter hours (GPA= QPTS/ QHRS).</p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> Where do I find a campus map? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>See a full <a href="http://campusmap.ucr.edu/imap/index.html">campus map here</a>. </p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> Where do I find a building map? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>See a full <a href="http://campusmap.ucr.edu/imap/index.html">campus map here</a>. </p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> Where do I find a map of classrooms? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>See a full <a href="http://campusmap.ucr.edu/imap/index.html">campus map here</a>. </p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> How do I find my class? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>Refer to the full <a href="http://campusmap.ucr.edu/imap/index.html">campus map here</a> to find the building where your classroom is located. </p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> I need to find a building. 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>See a full <a href="http://campusmap.ucr.edu/imap/index.html">campus map here</a>. </p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> My club or organization needs a room for a meeting/event. How do I get one? How do I reserve a room? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>You can reserve a room through <a href="http://www.highlanderunionbuilding.ucr.edu/EventScheduling/Pages/CommonsEventScheduling.aspx" target="_blank">Highlander Event Scheduling</a>. </p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> When are finals? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>Please see the <a href="../academic-calendar/final-exam-schedule.aspx">Final Exam Schedule. </a></p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> Where is the Academic Calendar? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p><a href="../academic-calendar/Default.aspx">Right here. </a></p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> How do I obtain a copy of a course description? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>Catalogs from 1998 and to the present can be found on <a href="http://registrar.ucr.edu/registrar/archives/default.aspx">Archives page of the Registrar</a> site to view or print out past course descriptions. Descriptions needed for academic years prior to 1998 should be directed <a href="mailto: reghelpdesk@ucr.edu">reghelpdesk@ucr.edu</a> or 951-827-7284. </p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> How do I change my major? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>Major changes are processed within colleges. Follow the links below for instructions. <br /> <a href="http://chassstudentaffairs.ucr.edu/majors_minors/index.html#changing">Changing majors to/from/within CHASS</a> <a href="http://cnasstudent.ucr.edu/majors/MajorSelection.html"><br /> Changing majors to/from/within CNAS</a><br /><a href="http://student.engr.ucr.edu/policies/requirements/majorchange.html">Changing majors to/from/within BCOE </a><a href="http://undergradbusiness.ucr.edu/major/applyingforbusiness.html"><br />Changing majors to/from/within SoBA </a></p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> How do I change my name? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>Please see <a href="../transcripts-grades-and-academic-records/change-of-name-or-address.aspx">Change of Name, Address or Phone Number.</a></p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> How do I change my phone number? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>Please see <a href="../transcripts-grades-and-academic-records/change-of-name-or-address.aspx">Change of Name, Address or Phone Number.</a></p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> How do I change my address? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>Please see <a href="../transcripts-grades-and-academic-records/change-of-name-or-address.aspx">Change of Name, Address or Phone Number.</a></p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> I lost my student status, what do I do? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>Please see <a href="../registering-for-classes/loss-of-course-lapse-status.aspx">Loss of Course/Lapse Status.</a></p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> Can I earn UCR credit through other programs? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>Please see <a href="../registering-for-classes/special-programs.aspx">Special Programs.</a></p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> Can I earn transfer credit? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>Please see <a href="../registering-for-classes/special-programs.aspx">Special Programs.</a></p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> Where can I find Registrar forms? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p><a href="../../registrar/forms/default.aspx">Right here. </a></p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> Where is the Office of the Registrar? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>Our office is located on the second floor of the Student Services Building, Room 2249. For in-person service, students should start at the Highlander One Stop Shop (HOSS) on the first floor of the Student Services Building. Office hours are Monday through Friday, 9 a.m. to 5 p.m. </p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> Where is your office? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>Our office is located on the second floor of the Student Services Building, room 2249. For in-person service, students should start at the Highlander One Stop Shop (HOSS) on the first floor of the Student Services Building. Office hours are Monday through Friday, 9 a.m. to 5 p.m. </p> 
       </dd>

       </dd> 
       <a class="btt" href="#top">Back to Top</a> 
      </dl> 
      <h4 class="section2 ms-alternating" id="section-8">FERPA</h4> 
      <dl> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> Who do I talk to about FERPA? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>Contact UCR’s FERPA Compliance Officer at (951) 827-3427. </p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> How do I change my FERPA privacy? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>Please see <a href="../privacy-ferpa/disclosure-policies.aspx">Disclosure Policies. </a></p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> How do I change my directory information? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>Please see <a href="../privacy-ferpa/disclosure-policies.aspx">Disclosure Policies. </a></p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> How do I make my information private? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>Please see <a href="../privacy-ferpa/disclosure-policies.aspx">Disclosure Policies. </a></p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> How can I get a copy of my student's grades? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>Your student can give that information directly (e.g. print or email you a copy of their records) or they can set you up as an “authorized user” on their Growl account. <a href="../privacy-ferpa/disclosure-policies.aspx">See How.</a></p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> If I'm paying for my child's education, why can't I get a copy of his records 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>According to FERPA, a student’s records do not belong to the person paying for the student’s education – they belong to the student. Information is only shared with the student’s consent, in a health or safety emergency or pursuant to another FERPA exception. Your child may grant you permission to access their records in many ways. Please see our <a href="../privacy-ferpa/disclosure-policies.aspx">Disclosure Policies </a>for details.</p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> Can you email me a transcript? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>We never release confidential information over the phone or by email. See our <a href="../transcripts-grades-and-academic-records/request-transcript.aspx">Request a Transcript</a> page for ways to obtain one.</p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> What records can authorized users see in Growl? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>Students can tailor what is seen. They can set it up so users can see their billing statements, financial aid information, grades and class schedule. They can also request that email reminders (including billing reminders) are sent directly to email accounts. Students can also use Growl to grant permission to speak with Financial Aid, Housing, and Student Business Services about accounts.</p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> Does UCR have a blanket release form? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p> UCR does not have a blanket release form covering the release of all student information to you. Release forms are generally very specific and students may be required to fill out department-specific <a href="../privacy-ferpa/disclosure-policies.aspx">authorization forms</a> each time they request information be shared with you. </p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> Can I access my student’s medical and/or counseling records? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>Not necessarily, unless it is an emergency. However, your student may be able to grant you access via specific release forms. Questions about medical records should be directed to the Campus Health Center and questions about counseling records should be directed to the Counseling Center.</p> 
       </dd> 
       <a class="btt" href="#top">Back to Top</a> 
      </dl> 
      <h4 class="section2 ms-alternating" id="section-9">Graduation</h4> 
      <dl> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> How do I forward my email (R’mail) after I graduate? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>Directions for forwarding your R’mail <a href="https://support.google.com/mail/answer/10957?hl=en">can be found here.</a> Your R’mail and Growl account do remain active and accessible after you have graduated. </p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> Can I access R’Mail after I graduate? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>You may want to forward your R’mail to a personal email account so that you don’t miss your diploma notice or other important UCR communications. However, your R’mail and Growl account do remain active and accessible after you have graduated. </p> 
       </dd>
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> Can I get into Growl after I graduate? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>Yes. Your Growl account remains active and accessible after you have graduated. </p> 
       </dd> 
       <dt> 
        <span class="icon"></span> Do I have to apply for graduation? 
       </dt> 
       <dd style="display: none"> 
        <p>Yes. Please see <a href="../guide-to-graduation/graduation-application-deadlines.aspx">Graduation Application Deadlines.</a></p> 
       </dd> 
       <a class="btt" href="#top">Back to Top</a> 
      </dl> 
     </div>

   <div id="content"> 
    <h2>Financial Performance and Rate Monitoring</h2> 
    <!-- Start Sidebar --> 
    <div id="sidebar"> 
     <div class="nav"> 
      <h3 class="accessibility">Main Navigation</h3> 
      <ul> 
       <li><a href="/" title="Home">Home<br /><span></span></a></li>

       <li><a href="/student_fees.html" title="Student Fees">Student Fees</a></li>
       <li><a href="/facilities_admin_cost_recover.html" title="Facilities and Administrative Cost Recovery">Facilities and Administrative Cost Recovery</a></li>
       <li class="currentpage"><h3><dfn>Current page is: </dfn>Financial Performance and Rate Monitoring</h3>
        <ul>
         <li><a href="/fprm/auxiliary.html" title="Auxiliary Enterprises">Auxiliary Enterprises</a></li>
         <li><a href="/fprm/sales_and_service.html" title="Sales &amp; Service Activities">Sales &amp; Service Activities</a></li>
         <li><a href="/fprm/graduate.html" title="Self-Supporting Graduate Degree Programs">Self-Supporting Graduate Degree Programs</a></li>

       <li><a href="/policies.html" title="Policies, Procedures and Forms">Policies, Procedures and Forms</a></li>

     </div> 
     <p><a href="/student_fees.html" class="img_link" onfocus="if(this.blur)this.blur()"><img alt="Student Fees" src="/images/StudentFees_quick_launch.png" /></a> </p> 
    </div> 
    <hr /> 
    <!-- End Sidebar --> 
    <!-- Start Content Area --> 
    <div id="main"> 
     <!-- com.omniupdate.editor csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/macy-wide.css" cssmenu="" width="992" --> 
     <!-- com.omniupdate.div label="title" group="Everyone" button="734" -->
     <!-- com.omniupdate.editor csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/style.css" cssmenu="/z-omniupdate/css/style.txt" width="700" toolbar="TITLE" --> 
     <!-- /com.omniupdate.div --> 
     <!-- com.omniupdate.div label="maincontent" group="Everyone" button="707" -->
     <!-- com.omniupdate.editor toolbar="IMG_ONLY" csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/style.css" cssmenu="/z-omniupdate/css/style.txt" width="700" -->
     <p><img class="color_bar" src="/images/FinancialPerformanceRateMonitoring.png" alt="Financial Performance and Rate Monitoring" width="700" height="140" /></p>
     <!-- /com.omniupdate.div --> 
     <!-- com.omniupdate.div label="center_col" group="Everyone" button="707" -->
     <!-- com.omniupdate.editor csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/style.css" cssmenu="/z-omniupdate/css/style.txt" width="460" -->
     <p>This section applies to those units on campus operating self-supporting businesses and to individuals having an interest in them. Businesses such as these do not have the benefit of being directly funded with State or Federal money. Instead, these units must balance sales expectations with operating costs which makes their activities uniquely challenging.</p> 
     <p>These business activities have been divided into distinct areas containing relevant forms, letters, policies, and other materials used in monitoring financial performance and rate development.</p> 
     <ul> 
      <li><a href="/fprm/auxiliary.html">Auxiliary Enterprises</a></li> 
      <li><a href="/fprm/sales_and_service.html">Sales &amp; Service Activities</a></li> 
      <li><a href="/fprm/graduate.html">Self-Supporting Graduate Degree Programs</a></li> 
      <li><a href="/fprm/general.html">General Business, Other Fee, and Assessments</a></li> 
      <li><a href="/fprm/insurance.html">Insurance</a></li> 
      <li><a href="/fprm/investment_performance.html">Cash Management and Investments</a></li> 
      <li><a href="/fprm/links.html">Policies and Useful Links</a></li> 
     </ul>
